<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[



/* JQUERY */
jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
    
   
  

	/* jQuery('ul#rmenu').superfish(); */
	/* jQuery('ul#rmenu').superfish().find('ul').bgIframe({opacity:false}); */
 
	/* For IE6 */
	if (jQuery.browser.msie && /MSIE 6\.0/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && !/MSIE 7\.0/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && !/MSIE 8\.0/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent)) {

		/* Max-width for images in IE6 */		
		var centerwidth = jQuery("td#middle").width(); 
		
		/* Images without caption */
		jQuery(".post img").each(function() { 
			var maxwidth = centerwidth - 10 + 'px';
			var imgwidth = jQuery(this).width(); 
			var imgheight = jQuery(this).height(); 
			var newimgheight = (centerwidth / imgwidth * imgheight) + 'px';	
			if (imgwidth > centerwidth) { 
				jQuery(this).css({width: maxwidth}); 
				jQuery(this).css({height: newimgheight}); 
			}
		});
		
		/* Images with caption */
		jQuery("div.wp-caption").each(function() { 
			var captionwidth = jQuery(this).width(); 
			var maxcaptionwidth = centerwidth + 'px';
			var captionheight = jQuery(this).height();
			var captionimgwidth =  jQuery("div.wp-caption img").width();
			var captionimgheight =  jQuery("div.wp-caption img").height();
			if (captionwidth > centerwidth) { 
				jQuery(this).css({width: maxcaptionwidth}); 
				var newcaptionheight = (centerwidth / captionwidth * captionheight) + 'px';
				var newcaptionimgheight = (centerwidth / captionimgwidth * captionimgheight) + 'px';
				jQuery(this).css({height: newcaptionheight}); 
				jQuery("div.wp-caption img").css({height: newcaptionimgheight}); 
				}
		});
		
		/* sfhover for LI:HOVER support in IE6: */
		jQuery("ul li").
			hover( function() {
					jQuery(this).addClass("sfhover")
				}, 
				function() {
					jQuery(this).removeClass("sfhover")
				} 
			); 

	/* End IE6 */
	}
	
	
	
	/* Since 3.7.8: Auto resize videos (embed and iframe elements) 
	TODO: Parse parent's dimensions only once per layout column, not per video
	*/
	function bfa_resize_video() {
		jQuery('embed, iframe').each( function() {
			var video = jQuery(this),
			videoWidth = video.attr('width'); // use the attr here, not width() or css()
			videoParent = video.parent(),
			videoParentWidth = parseFloat( videoParent.css( 'width' ) ),
			videoParentBorder = parseFloat( videoParent.css( 'border-left-width' ) ) 
										+  parseFloat( videoParent.css( 'border-right-width' ) ),
			videoParentPadding = parseFloat( videoParent.css( 'padding-left' ) ) 
										+  parseFloat( videoParent.css( 'padding-right' ) ),
			maxWidth = videoParentWidth - videoParentBorder - videoParentPadding;

			if( videoWidth > maxWidth ) {
				var videoHeight = video.attr('height'),
				videoMaxHeight = ( maxWidth / videoWidth * videoHeight );
				video.attr({ width: maxWidth, height: videoMaxHeight });
			} 

		});	
	}
	bfa_resize_video();
	jQuery(window).resize( bfa_resize_video );

		
	jQuery(".post table tr").
		mouseover(function() {
			jQuery(this).addClass("over");
		}).
		mouseout(function() {
			jQuery(this).removeClass("over");
		});

	
	jQuery(".post table tr:even").
		addClass("alt");

	
	jQuery("input.text, input.TextField, input.file, input.password, textarea").
		focus(function () {  
			jQuery(this).addClass("highlight"); 
		}).
		blur(function () { 
			jQuery(this).removeClass("highlight"); 
		})
	
	jQuery("input.inputblur").
		focus(function () {  
			jQuery(this).addClass("inputfocus"); 
		}).
		blur(function () { 
			jQuery(this).removeClass("inputfocus"); 
		})

		

	
	jQuery("input.button, input.Button, input#submit").
		mouseover(function() {
			jQuery(this).addClass("buttonhover");
		}).
		mouseout(function() {
			jQuery(this).removeClass("buttonhover");
		});

	/* toggle "you can use these xhtml tags" */
	jQuery("a.xhtmltags").
		click(function(){ 
			jQuery("div.xhtml-tags").slideToggle(300); 
		});

	/* For the Tabbed Widgets plugin: */
	jQuery("ul.tw-nav-list").
		addClass("clearfix");

		
	
});

//]]>
</script>

								<div class="post-84 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-cpp-tutorial odd" id="post-84">
						<div class="post-headline">		<h1>6.3 &#8212; Arrays and loops</h1>
		</div>		<div class="post-byline">By Alex, on July 2nd, 2007</div>		<div class="post-bodycopy clearfix"><p><strong>Loops and arrays</strong></p>
<p>Because array elements can be accessed by a variable, it is common to use a loop to access or manipulate each array element in turn.  Wherever you find arrays, you will almost certainly find loops as well.</p>
<p>Consider the case where we want to find the average test score of a class of students.  Using individual variables:</p>
<p></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

		<div id="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-familiar-learncppcom crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" no-popup minimize scroll-mouseover wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"></div>
			<div class="crayon-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="crayon-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-1">1</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-2">2</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-3">3</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-4">4</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-5">5</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-6">6</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-7">7</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-8">8</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-9">9</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-1"><span class="crayon-m">const</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore0</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">84</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-3"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore1</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">92</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-4"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore2</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">76</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-5"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore3</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">81</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-6"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore4</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">56</span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nTotalScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore0</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore1</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore2</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore3</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nScore4</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c68ee666182571-9"><span class="crayon-t">double</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">dAverageScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-r">static_cast</span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-t">double</span><span class="crayon-o">&gt;</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">nTotalScore</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">/</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0025 seconds] -->
<p></p>
<p>That&#8217;s a lot of variables and a lot of typing -- and this is just 5 students!  Imagine how much work we&#8217;d have to do for 30 students, or 150.  </p>
<p>Plus, if a new student is added, a new variable has to be declared, initialized, and added to the nTotalScore calculation.  Any time you have to adjust old code, you run the risk of introducing errors.</p>
<p>Using arrays without loops offers a slightly better solution:</p>
<p></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

		<div id="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-familiar-learncppcom crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" no-popup minimize scroll-mouseover wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"></div>
			<div class="crayon-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="crayon-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340-1">1</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340-2">2</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340-3">3</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340-4">4</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340-1"><span class="crayon-m">const</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340-2"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">{</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">84</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">92</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">76</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">81</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">56</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">}</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340-3"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nTotalScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-cn">1</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-cn">2</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-cn">3</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-cn">4</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6900140938340-4"><span class="crayon-t">double</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">dAverageScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-r">static_cast</span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-t">double</span><span class="crayon-o">&gt;</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">nTotalScore</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">/</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0024 seconds] -->
<p></p>
<p>This cuts down on the number of variables declared significantly, but nTotalScore still requires each array element be listed individually.  Furthermore, changing the number of students means the nTotalScore formula needs to be adjusted.</p>
<p>Using arrays with loops:</p>
<p></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

		<div id="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-familiar-learncppcom crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" no-popup minimize scroll-mouseover wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"></div>
			<div class="crayon-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="crayon-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-1">1</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-2">2</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-3">3</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-4">4</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-5">5</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-6">6</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-7">7</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-1"><span class="crayon-m">const</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-2"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">{</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">84</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">92</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">76</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">81</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">56</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">}</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-3"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nTotalScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-4"><span class="crayon-st">for</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-o">++</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-5"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">nTotalScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">+=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-6">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6908774248984-7"><span class="crayon-t">double</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">dAverageScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-r">static_cast</span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-t">double</span><span class="crayon-o">&gt;</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">nTotalScore</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">/</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0024 seconds] -->
<p></p>
<p>This solution is ideal in terms of both readability and maintenance.  Because the loop does all of our array element accesses, the formulas adjust automatically to account for the number of elements in the array.  This means the formulas do not have to be manually altered to account for new students, and we do not have to manually enter the name of each array element!</p>
<p>Here&#8217;s another example of using a loop with an array to determine the best score in the class:</p>
<p></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

		<div id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-familiar-learncppcom crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" no-popup minimize scroll-mouseover wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"></div>
			<div class="crayon-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="crayon-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-1">1</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-2">2</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-3">3</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-4">4</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-5">5</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-6">6</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-7">7</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-8">8</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-1"><span class="crayon-m">const</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-2"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">{</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">84</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">92</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">76</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">81</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">56</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">}</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-3"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nMaxScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-4"><span class="crayon-st">for</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nNumStudents</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-o">++</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-5"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-st">if</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&gt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nMaxScore</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-6"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">nMaxScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anScores</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">nStudent</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-7">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6910865188807-8"><span class="crayon-r">cout</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"The best score was "</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nMaxScore</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">endl</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0027 seconds] -->
<p></p>
<p>In this example, we use a non-loop variable called nMaxScore.  nMaxScore is initialized to 0 to represent that we have not seen any scores yet.  We then iterate through each element of the array, and if we find a score that is higher than any we&#8217;ve seen before, we set nMaxScore to that value.  Thus, nMaxScore always represents the best score out of all the elements we&#8217;ve searched so far.  By the time we reach the end of the array, nMaxScore holds the highest score in the entire array.</p>
<p>Loops are typically used with arrays to do one of three things:<br />
1) Search for a value (eg. highest, lowest).<br />
2) Calculate a value (eg. average, total)<br />
3) Reorganize the array (eg. sort from lowest to highest)</p>
<p>When searching for a value, a variable is typically used to hold the best candidate value seen so far (or the array index of the best candidate).  In the above example where we use a loop to find the best score, this variable is used to hold the highest score encountered so far.</p>
<p>When calculating a value, a variable is typically used to hold an intermediate result that is used to calculate the final value.  In the above example where we are calculating an average score, nTotalScore holds the total score for all the elements examined so far.  This value is then later used to calculate the overall average score.</p>
<p>Sorting an array is a bit more tricky, as it typically involves nested loops.  We will cover sorting an array in the next lesson.</p>
<p><strong>Off-by-one errors</strong></p>
<p>One of the trickiest parts of using loops with arrays is making sure the loop iterates the proper number of times.  Off-by-one errors are easy to make, and trying to access an element that is larger than the size of the array can have dire consequences.  Consider the following program:</p>
<p></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

		<div id="crayon-555d7567c6919630492992" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-familiar-learncppcom crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" no-popup minimize scroll-mouseover wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"></div>

				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6919630492992-1"><span class="crayon-m">const</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nArraySize</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6919630492992-2"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">{</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">6</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">8</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">2</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">4</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">9</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">}</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6919630492992-3"><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6919630492992-4"><span class="crayon-st">for</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nIndex</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nIndex</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-st">if</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">anArray</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">nIndex</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&gt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nMaxValue</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6919630492992-6"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">nMaxValue</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anArray</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">nIndex</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>

<!-- [Format Time: 0.0024 seconds] -->
<p></p>
<p>The problem with this program is that the conditional in the for loop is wrong!  The array declared has 5 elements, indexed from 0 to 4.  However, this array loops from 0 to 5.  Consequently, on the last iteration, the array will execute this:</p>
<p></p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

		<div id="crayon-555d7567c6920878298477" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-familiar-learncppcom crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" no-popup minimize scroll-mouseover wrap" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"></div>
			<div class="crayon-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="crayon-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="crayon-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6920878298477-1">1</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="crayon-555d7567c6920878298477-2">2</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6920878298477-1"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-st">if</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">anArray</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&gt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nMaxValue</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c6920878298477-2"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">nMaxValue</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anArray</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0007 seconds] -->
<p></p>
<p>But anArray[5] is undefined!  This can cause all sorts of issues, with the most likely being that anArray[5] results in a garbage value.  In this case, the probable result is that nMaxValue will be wrong.</p>
<p>However, imagine what would happen if we inadvertently assigned a value to anArray[5]!  We might overwrite another variable (or part of it), or perhaps corrupt something -- these types of bugs can be very hard to track down!</p>
<p>Consequently, when using loops with arrays, always double-check your loop conditions to make sure you do not introduce off-by-one errors.</p>

class="crayon-r">cout</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">anArray</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">iii</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">" "</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567c692e065119881-8"><span class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567c692e065119881-9"><span class="crayon-sy">}</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0025 seconds] -->

		<p>If you mean this:</p><!-- Crayon Syntax Highlighter v2.7.1 -->

				</td>
						<td class="crayon-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567cb520950774942-1"><span class="crayon-st">for</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">count</span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">count</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">9</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">count</span><span class="crayon-o">--</span><span class="crayon-o">-</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div></div></td>

<!-- [Format Time: 0.0007 seconds] -->
<p></p>
<p>The answer is that it doesn&#8217;t work because you have three minuses instead of two.  Two minuses means &#8220;decrement the value of count by 1&#8243;.  Three minuses is meaningless -- and it&#8217;s invalid syntax in C  .  That&#8217;s why it&#8217;s giving you a syntax error.</p>
		</div>

		<p>Your code is not quite correct -- what happens if it doesn&#8217;t find the number the user entered?  In that case, iii will be 10 when the loop exits, and your code will still print that the number has index 10, which is not a valid index.</p>
<p>As an aside, using a for loop to iterate through an array is usually better than a while loop because it contains the initialization and increment all within one statement, making it less likely you&#8217;ll forget them.</p>
		</div>

<ul class="children">
		<li class="comment byuser comment-author-alex bypostauthor odd alt depth-2 clearfix" id="comment-14667">
		<div id="div-comment-14667" class="clearfix comment-container bypostauthor">
		<div class="comment-author vcard">
		<img alt='' src='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/a4e62d28c29f6c864923207d4c17993b?s=65&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/a4e62d28c29f6c864923207d4c17993b?s=130&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-65 photo' height='65' width='65' />		<span class="authorname"><a href='http://www.tarindel.com' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Alex</a></span>
		</div>
				<div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
		<a href="http://www.learncpp.com/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/#comment-14667">
		May 5, 2008 at 9:02 pm</a>
        <span class="comment-reply-link"><a class='comment-reply-link' href='/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/?replytocom=14667#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-14667", "14667", "respond", "84" )' aria-label='Reply to Alex'> &middot; Reply</a></span>		 
		</div>
		<p>In C++, all arrays are 0-based, meaning the first element is numbered 0.  In regular life, if we have 9 items, we&#8217;d count them like this: 1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8 9.  However, in C++, we begin counting at 0, so we count 9 items like this: 0 1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8.  That&#8217;s why the array is indexed 0 to 8.</p>
		</div>

		<li class="comment byuser comment-author-alex bypostauthor even depth-2 clearfix" id="comment-30003">
		<div id="div-comment-30003" class="clearfix comment-container bypostauthor">
		<div class="comment-author vcard">
		<img alt='' src='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/a4e62d28c29f6c864923207d4c17993b?s=65&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/a4e62d28c29f6c864923207d4c17993b?s=130&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-65 photo' height='65' width='65' />		<span class="authorname"><a href='http://www.tarindel.com' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Alex</a></span>
		</div>
				<div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
		<a href="http://www.learncpp.com/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/#comment-30003">
		October 14, 2008 at 6:31 pm</a>
        <span class="comment-reply-link"><a class='comment-reply-link' href='/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/?replytocom=30003#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-30003", "30003", "respond", "84" )' aria-label='Reply to Alex'> &middot; Reply</a></span>		 
		</div>
		<p>anArray[5] won&#8217;t cause a compiler error, and it IS dangerous.  C++ does not do any sort of compile-time bounds checking on it&#8217;s arrays -- and perhaps worse, it doesn&#8217;t do any runtime bounds checking either!  This is one of those areas that definitely falls under &#8220;trust the programmer&#8221;.</p>
<p>The underlying reason is due to the fact that arrays are implemented as pointers, and [] is implemented as a pointer addition operation.  You&#8217;ll learn more about this in lesson 6.8.</p>
<p>Once you learn about C++ classes, you&#8217;ll be able to write your own array classes that look and feel exactly like C++ built-in arrays, but can have additional safety features like runtime range checking.</p>
		</div>
</li><!-- #comment-## -->
</ul><!-- .children -->

id="crayon-555d7567cae80322870070-8"><span class="crayon-h">	</span><span class="crayon-st">if</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span 					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>

<p></p>

</span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">nUserNum</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;&lt;</span><span class="crayon-line" id="crayon-555d7567cace0835213339-27"><span class="crayon-h">	</span><span class="crayon-st">return</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">;</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-555d7567cace0835213339-28"><span class="crayon-sy">}</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>
<!-- [Format Time: 0.0049 seconds] -->
<p></p>
<p>It&#8217;s just wrong to try to do too many things with one variable. ?</p>
<p>It left me baffled for a while because most user inputs would print the correct element!</p>
		</div>
<ul class="children">
		<li class="comment byuser comment-author-alex bypostauthor even depth-2 clearfix" id="comment-34215">
		<div id="div-comment-34215" class="clearfix comment-container bypostauthor">
		<div class="comment-author vcard">
		<img alt='' src='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/a4e62d28c29f6c864923207d4c17993b?s=65&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/a4e62d28c29f6c864923207d4c17993b?s=130&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-65 photo' height='65' width='65' />		<span class="authorname"><a href='http://www.tarindel.com' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Alex</a></span>
		</div>
				<div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
		<a href="http://www.learncpp.com/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/#comment-34215">
		December 10, 2008 at 11:50 pm</a>
        <span class="comment-reply-link"><a class='comment-reply-link' href='/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/?replytocom=34215#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-34215", "34215", "respond", "84" )' aria-label='Reply to Alex'> &middot; Reply</a></span>		 
		</div>
		<p>Yup, generally speaking it&#8217;s good to have a variable keep track of one and only one thing.  Here, your nUserNum has two jobs: to accept the user input, and then later to store the index of the matching array element, which is a totally different thing!</p>
<p>Although it may have taken you a while to find and fix the issue, it&#8217;s a good lesson to learn.</p>
		</div>

		December 22, 2008 at 11:23 pm</a>
        <span class="comment-reply-link"><a class='comment-reply-link' href='/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/?replytocom=35426#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-35426", "35426", "respond", "84" )' aria-label='Reply to Alex'> &middot; Reply</a></span>		 
		</div>
		<p>What do you mean &#8220;which comes first?&#8221;</p>
<p>The program executes sequentially.  You can think of it as being 3 parts.</p>
<p>First is the do-while.  The do-while executes until the while is false.</p>
<p>Second is the for iii loop.  This loop executes until iii >= 9.</p>
<p>Third is the for jjj loop.  This loop executes until jjj >= 9.</p>

		<p>I dont know about Visual C++ 2005, but on Visual C++ 2008, the code on the second quiz does not seem to work right. I am using the professional edition of Visual Studio 2008 so it might be different for some people. The error on the program is that when it identifies the index it is allways off by one. For example if I type 4, this will be the following output:</p>
<p>7<br />
4 6 7 3 8 2 1 9 5</p>
<p>The number 4 has index 2</p>
<p>The index output in the 4th line is always decreased by 1. If you are expirencing the same problem, please try to use this code instead. It has the increment statement added in a certain point that increases the index value to the right amount (or you could use &#8220;jjj += 1;&#8221; statement but I used incrementation). And its aloways a good idea to make sure the program doesn&#8217;t automatically close (the &#8220;break;&#8221; statement is now used only for just in case):</p>

		<div class="comment-author vcard">
		<img alt='' src='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/af6d64579f9acd6521a081e46729ca70?s=65&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/af6d64579f9acd6521a081e46729ca70?s=130&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-65 photo' height='65' width='65' />		<span class="authorname">Sagar</span>

		December 27, 2009 at 3:45 pm</a>
        <span class="comment-reply-link"><a class='comment-reply-link' href='/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/?replytocom=74973#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-74973", "74973", "respond", "84" )' aria-label='Reply to Sagar'> &middot; Reply</a></span>		 
		</div>
		<p>[code] In solution number 2, shouldn&#8217;t it be nNumber &gt; 1 || nNumber &lt; 9 ?</p>
		</div>
<ul class="children">
		<li class="comment even depth-2 clearfix" id="comment-251213">
		<div id="div-comment-251213" class="clearfix comment-container">
		<div class="comment-author vcard">
		<img alt='' src='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/a4f878dc8e3118529a9e9929fd6d5933?s=65&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/a4f878dc8e3118529a9e9929fd6d5933?s=130&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-65 photo' height='65' width='65' />		<span class="authorname">Sergio Ramos</span>
		</div>
				<div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
		<a href="http://www.learncpp.com/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/#comment-251213">
		January 21, 2015 at 9:36 pm</a>
        <span class="comment-reply-link"><a class='comment-reply-link' href='/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/?replytocom=251213#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-251213", "251213", "respond", "84" )' aria-label='Reply to Sergio Ramos'> &middot; Reply</a></span>		 
		</div>
		<p>No because that&#8217;s how the &#8220;Do While&#8221; loop works. A &#8220;Do While&#8221; loop will perform the &#8220;Do&#8221; statement (the request for a number 1 to 9) so long as it&#8217;s condition is true. So you want it to be false.</p>
<p>Say, if nNumber is less than 1 or greater than 9, the entire condition will be true and the &#8220;Do While&#8221; statement will repeat, until the entire condition becomes false. !(9) or  (&gt;1 &amp;&amp; &lt;9). </p>
<p>Review the &quot;De Morgans law&quot; section of &quot;3.6 - Logical Operators&quot; for further information.</p>
		</div>
</li><!-- #comment-## -->
</ul><!-- .children -->
</li><!-- #comment-## -->

		<p>Hey  - the below code is copy pasted directly from Microsoft Visual 2010 and as far as i can see its exactly the same as the solution Alex posted. </p>
<p>I&#8217;m new to learning c++, and I&#8217;m really enjoying following this tutorial. </p>
<p>My question is this:<br />
When i run the program it correctly keeps asking for a number between 1 and 9 as long as i input a number when prompted. However if I input a letter (Tried it to see what would happen incase of a misstype) it seems to go into an endless loop. Is it supposed to do that (with the code written) or is there another way to avoid this problem I should implement?</p>

		<div class="comment-author vcard">
		<img alt='' src='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/3e62221422bd60ab4a95205ccb95c4f6?s=65&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/3e62221422bd60ab4a95205ccb95c4f6?s=130&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-65 photo' height='65' width='65' />		<span class="authorname">Slotenmaker</span>

		February 16, 2013 at 7:33 pm</a>
        <span class="comment-reply-link"><a class='comment-reply-link' href='/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/?replytocom=98189#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-98189", "98189", "respond", "84" )' aria-label='Reply to Slotenmaker'> &middot; Reply</a></span>		 
		</div>
		<p>I had the same problem, it is because of cin.<br />
cin tries to stream a character inside an integer, which will fail. But the stream will stay in memory! So the next loop it will again try the same character, and again, and again, etc.</p>
<p>If you put this code in the while loop it fixes this problem, you will also have to #include .<br />
It clears the stream:</p>
<p><code>cin.clear();<br />
      cin.ignore(numeric_limits&lt;streamsize&gt;::max(), &#039;\n&#039;);</code></p>
<p>Also you can use strings as an alternative.</p>
		</div>

		<p>hi people&#8230; i&#8217;ve written some codes to compose a multiplying equation that consist of every integer from 1 to 9.<br />
anybody have any idea to simplify my codes so that it won&#8217;t look so messy?</p>
<p>#include &#8220;stdafx.h&#8221;<br />
#include </p>
<p>int main()<br />
	{<br />
		using namespace std;</p>
<p>		int anX[9];</p>
<p>	    for(anX[0]=1; anX[0]&lt;5; anX[0]++)<br />
			{<br />
				for(anX[1]=1; anX[1]&lt;10; anX[1]++)<br />
					{<br />
						if(anX[0]==anX[1])<br />
							continue;<br />
						for(anX[2]=1; anX[2]&lt;10; anX[2]++)<br />
							{<br />
								if(anX[1]==anX[2])<br />
									continue;<br />
								for(anX[3]=1; anX[3]&lt;10; anX[3]++)<br />
									{<br />
										if(anX[2]==anX[3])<br />
											continue;<br />
										for(anX[4]=1; anX[4] 9999 || aaa &lt; 1000)<br />
															continue;<br />
														anX[5] = aaa/1000;<br />
														anX[6] = (aaa - anX[5]*1000)/100;<br />
														anX[7] = (aaa - anX[5]*1000 - anX[6]*100)/10;<br />
														anX[8] = aaa - anX[5]*1000 - anX[6]*100 - anX[7]*10;<br />
														if(anX[5]==0 || anX[6]==0 || anX[7]==0 || anX[8]==0)<br />
															continue;<br />
														bool result = true;</p>
<p>														for(int iii=0; iii&lt;9; iii++)<br />
															for(int jjj=0; jjj&lt;9; jjj++)<br />
																{<br />
																	if(iii!=jjj &amp;&amp; anX[iii]==anX[jjj])<br />
																		result = false;<br />
																}<br />
															if(result)<br />
																{<br />
																	cout &lt;&lt; &quot;The Result is?&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;<br />
																	int bbb = anX[0]*1000 + anX[1]*100 + anX[2]*10 + anX[3];<br />
																	int ccc = bbb * anX[4];<br />
																	cout &lt;&lt; bbb &lt;&lt; &quot; * &quot; &lt;&lt; anX[4] &lt;&lt; &quot; = &quot; &lt;&lt; ccc &lt;&lt; endl;<br />
																}<br />
													}<br />
											}<br />
									}<br />
							}<br />
					}<br />
			}<br />
			cout &lt;&lt; &quot;The End?&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;<br />
	}</p>
		</div>
</li><!-- #comment-## -->

		</div>
		<p>I was under the impression I was supposed to print the array of numbers that the user gave as input instead of the given array in the example. Probably it is better do use do while loops instead of my solution, but this is what I came up with (unfortunately it seems &#8220;&lt;&lt;&quot; and include iostream seems to be messed up by the post):</p>
<p>#include </p>
<p>int main(int argc, const char * argv[])<br />
{<br />
    using namespace std;</p>
<p>    int anInputNumbers[200]={0};<br />
    int nCorrectInputIdx;</p>
<p>    for (int iii=0;iii&lt;200;iii++){<br />
        cout &lt;&gt; anInputNumbers[iii];<br />
        if (anInputNumbers[iii]&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; anInputNumbers[iii] &lt;=9){<br />
            nCorrectInputIdx=iii;<br />
            cout &lt;&lt; &quot;The numbers you entered were:&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;<br />
            for (int jjj=0;jjj&lt;=iii;jjj++)<br />
                cout &lt;&lt; anInputNumbers[jjj] &lt;&lt; &quot; &quot;;<br />
            cout &lt;&lt; endl &lt;&lt; &quot;You managed to enter a correct number on try &quot; &lt;&lt; nCorrectInputIdx+1 &lt;&lt; endl;<br />
            break;<br />
        }<br />
    }</p>
<p>    return 0;<br />
}</p>
		</div>
<ul class="children">

		<p><code><br />
#include &lt;iostream&gt;</p>
<p>int main(int argc, const char * argv[])<br />
{<br />
    using namespace std;</p>
<p>    int anInputNumbers[200]={0};<br />
    int nCorrectInputIdx;</p>
<p>    for (int iii=0;iii&lt;200;iii++){<br />
        cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Enter a number between 0-9: &quot;;<br />
        cin &gt;&gt; anInputNumbers[iii];<br />
        if (anInputNumbers[iii]&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; anInputNumbers[iii] &lt;=9){<br />
            nCorrectInputIdx=iii;<br />
            cout &lt;&lt; &quot;The numbers you entered were:&quot; &lt;&lt; endl;<br />
            for (int jjj=0;jjj&lt;=iii;jjj++)<br />
                cout &lt;&lt; anInputNumbers[jjj] &lt;&lt; &quot; &quot;;<br />
            cout &lt;&lt; endl &lt;&lt; &quot;You managed to enter a correct number on try &quot; &lt;&lt; nCorrectInputIdx+1 &lt;&lt; endl; // index plus one to get the number of tries<br />
            break;<br />
        }<br />
    }</p>
<p>    return 0;<br />
}</p>
<p></code></p>

		<img alt='' src='http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/ba9baac10b857f44b564dbd15c1afa0b?s=65&#038;d=mm&#038;r=g' srcset='http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/ba9baac10b857f44b564dbd15c1afa0b?s=130&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x' class='avatar avatar-65 photo' height='65' width='65' />		<span class="authorname"><a href='http://www.learncpp.com/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Cliff</a></span>
		</div>
				<div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
		<a href="http://www.learncpp.com/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/#comment-251767">
		March 10, 2015 at 10:48 am</a>
        <span class="comment-reply-link"><a class='comment-reply-link' href='/cpp-tutorial/63-arrays-and-loops/?replytocom=251767#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( "comment-251767", "251767", "respond", "84" )' aria-label='Reply to Cliff'> &middot; Reply</a></span>		 
		</div>
		<p>Regarding the problem in question #2, when a non-numeric character is entered, I found a solution by doing the while loop using character values then converting the character input to a numeric by substracting 48. See my code below:</p>
<p>//&nbsp;&nbsp;Created by Cliff on 3/10/15.<br />
//&nbsp;&nbsp;Copyright (c) 2015 Cliff. All rights reserved.<br />
//</p>
<p>#include &lt;iostream&gt;</p>
<p>int main() {<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;using namespace std;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;char cInput(0);<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;int anNumbers [9] {4,6,7,3,8,2,1,9,5};<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;//Get user input<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;do<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;{&nbsp;&nbsp; cout &lt;&lt; &quot; Please enter a number between 1 and 9 n&quot;;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cin &gt;&gt; cInput;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;while (cInput &lt; &#8216;1&#8217; || cInput &gt; &#8216;9&#8217;); //Using char type to keep from loop with non-numeric input.<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;// Print array<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for (int iii = 0; iii &lt; 9; iii++)<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cout &lt;&lt; anNumbers [iii] &lt;&lt; &quot; &quot;;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;// Search array for user entered number to get index value.<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;int jjj(0);<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cout &lt;&lt;endl;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for (jjj=0; anNumbers[jjj] != cInput - 48; jjj++)<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;// Print index<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cout &lt;&lt; jjj + 1 &lt;&lt; endl;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return 0;<br />
}</p>
		</div>
</li><!-- #comment-## -->
	
	</ul>
